[30;1m43 | [0m[35m[0m
[30;1m44 | [0m[35m  This follows the Nature DQN schedule of a linearly decaying epsilon (Mnih et[0m
[30;1m45 | [0m[35m  al., 2015). The schedule is as follows:[0m

[30;1m172 | [0m[35m[0m
[30;1m173 | [0m[35m  This follows the Nature DQN schedule of a linearly decaying epsilon (Mnih et[0m
[30;1m174 | [0m[35m  al., 2015). The schedule is as follows:[0m
[30;1m175 | [0m[35m    Begin at 1. until warmup_steps steps have been taken; then[0m
[30;1m176 | [0m[35m    Linearly decay epsilon from 1. to epsilon in decay_period steps; and then[0m
[30;1m177 | [0m[35m    Use epsilon from there on.[0m
